c init=
	400
	~	
	~		|

p init=
	8757
	~	
	~		|

f init=
	5075
	~	
	~		|

kf=
	( fi 0 + dnl b - gngf b ) / see b
	~	
	~		|

kp=
	( pi 0 - gngp b ) / see b
	~	
	~		|

gngf b=
	gngf end b + gngf ex b
	~	
	~		|

fetw=
	3/8
	~	
	~		|

cell mass b=
	1/fwcm * icw b
	~	
	~		|

fiew=
	(1-fetw)/fetw
	~	
	~		|

gngf ex b=
	exog glycerol per kcal fat intake * fi 0 * cal c
	~	
	~		|

see b=
	tee b - gngp b - gngf b
	~	
	~		|

pi 0=
	500
	~	
	~		|

eff c dnl b=
	1 / ( k dnl ^ hill dnl + 1 )
	~	
	~		|

fwcm=
	7/10
	~	
	~		|

ci 0=
	1500
	~	
	~		|

tee b=
	mei b
	~	
	~		|

fw=
	7/10
	~	
	~		|

dnl b=
	ci 0 * eff c dnl b
	~	
	~		|

z check 0=
	1+wpi+wci+wg+wf
	~	
	~		|

icw b=
	fiew * ecw b
	~	
	~		|

z check 1=
	wf/kf
	~	
	~		|

fi 0=
	1000
	~	
	~		|

kc=
	( ci 0 - dnl b ) / see b
	~	
	~		|

eff fox p= WITH LOOKUP (
	fox p / fox d,
		([(0,0)-(3,1)],(0,0),(0.4,0.4),(0.798165,0.627193),(1.30275,0.824561),(2,0.95),(3,1\
		) ))
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

fox p=
	f / TIME STEP * cal f
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

fox a=
	fox d / cal f * eff fox p
	~	g/Day
	~		|

pox s=
	fp s * gap / cal p
	~	g/Day
	~		|

pox s k=
	pox s * cal p
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

fox s k=
	fox s * cal f
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

ox=
	ox p + ox s
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

cox s=
	fc s * gap / cal c
	~	g/Day
	~		|

cox s k=
	cox s * cal c
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

fox s=
	ff s * gap / cal f
	~	g/Day
	~		|

d ox tee=
	IF THEN ELSE( ox - tee < 0.1, 0, ox - tee )
	~	kcal/Day [0,0.1]
	~		|

ox s=
	cox s k + fox s k + pox s k
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

y=
	prot term + is sufficient carb * carb term + is sufficient fat * fat term
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

fc s=
	is sufficient carb * carb term / y
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

ff s=
	is sufficient fat * fat term / y
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

fp s=
	prot term / y
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

is sufficient fat=
	IF THEN ELSE( gap f < 0.1 , 1 , 0 )
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

is sufficient carb=
	IF THEN ELSE( gap c < 0.1 , 1, 0 )
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

cox a=
	cox d / cal c * eff suff c
	~	g/Day
	~		|

cox d=
	fc * see + gngf + gngp
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

suff c=
	c * cal c / cox d
	~	Day
	~		|

eff suff c= WITH LOOKUP (
	suff c,
		([(0,0)-(1,1),(0,0),(0.1,0.6),(0.2,0.85),(0.3,0.95),(0.4,1),(1,1)],(0,0),(0.1,0.6),\
		(0.2,0.85),(0.3,0.95),(0.4,1),(1,1) ))
	~	Dmnl
	~	\!suff c
	|

gap=
	gap c + gap f
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

f= INTEG (
	+fi g-fox a+dnl i-gngf o-fox s,
		f init)
	~	g
	~		|

c= INTEG (
	ci g+gngf i+gngp i-cox a-dnl o-cox s,
		c init)
	~	g
	~		|

gap c=
	cox d - cox a * cal c
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

gap f=
	fox d - fox a * cal f
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

cox k=
	cox a * cal c
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

p= INTEG (
	pi g-gngp o-pox a-pox s,
		p init)
	~	g
	~		|

fox k=
	fox a * cal f
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

pox k=
	pox a * cal p
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

ox p=
	cox k + fox k + pox k
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

ec=
	-268
	~	kcal/Day
	~	double counted baseline metabolic activity
	|

rmr=
	mbc + mt + mc + ec
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

z=
	carb term + fat term +prot term
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

wf=
	(1 + wpi) * kf / kp
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

fat term=
	MAX( 0 , wf * ndf)
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

wg=
	kc / kp * ( 1 + wpi )- wci
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

eff dg cox=
	wg * ndc
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

eff act pox=
	sa * EXP( - LN(sa) * nacteng bw )
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

spi=
	15.0253
	~	Dmnl
	~	Makalede bu degiken 7.
	|

sa=
	4
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

eff pi pox=
	wpi * ( 1 + spi * ndpi )
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

eff ci cox=
	wci * ( 1 + sci * ndci )
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

wpi=
	0.1
	~	Dmnl
	~	relative rate of exogenous to endogenous protein in balanced state (from \
		model)
	|

prot term=
	( ndp + MAX( 0, eff pi pox )  ) * eff act pox
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

sci=
	0.761188
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

wci=
	3.31414
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

carb term=
	eff dg cox + MAX( 0 , eff ci cox * ( c / (0.1 + c) )  )
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

dnleff=
	0.8
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

gngeff=
	0.8
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

mc=
	( 1 - dnleff ) * dnl + ( 1- gngeff ) * ( gngf + gngp )
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

see=
	tee - gngp - gngf
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

dnl=
	ci g * eff c dnl * cal c
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

dnl o=
	min( dnl / cal c , c / TIME STEP )
	~	g/Day
	~		|

pox d=
	fp * see
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

gngf=
	gngf end + gngf ex
	~	
	~		|

fox d=
	ff * see
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

gngf i=
	gngf / cal c
	~	g/Day
	~		|

gngf o=
	min( gngf / cal f , f / TIME STEP )
	~	g/Day
	~		|

gngp o=
	MAX( 0 , gngp / cal p)
	~	g/Day
	~		|

dnl i=
	dnl / cal f
	~	g/Day
	~		|

gngp=
	MAX( 0 , gngp b * ( np - eff ci gngp + eff pi gngp ) )
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

eff ci gngp=
	0.506 * ndci
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

gngp i=
	gngp / cal c
	~	g/Day
	~		|

pox a=
	pox d / cal p
	~	g/Day
	~		|

gngf end b=
	df mol b * mass of glycerol * cal c
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

gngf end=
	gngf end b * ndf
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

gngf ex=
	exog glycerol per kcal fat intake * fi k * cal c
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

exog glycerol per kcal fat intake=
	mass of glycerol / ( cal f * mass tg )
	~	g/kcal
	~		|

hill dnl=
	4
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

k dnl=
	2
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

eff c dnl=
	nc ^ hill dnl / 
	( k dnl ^ hill dnl + nc ^ hill dnl )
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

dci=
	ci k - ci b
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

ndci=
	dci / ci b
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

ndpi=
	dpi / pi b
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

np=
	p / p b
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

dpi=
	pi k - pi b
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

eff pi gngp=
	0.306 * ndpi
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

gngp b=
	100
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

eff ci df=
	1 + ( ( lipol max - lipol min )  * EXP( -k lip * ci g * cal c / ci b )
	+ lipol min - 1 )
	/ MAX( 1 , eff obes df )
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

df=
	df mol b * ndf * mass tg
	~	g/Day
	~		|

tef=
	tef c * cal c * ci g + tef f * fi k + tef p * cal p * pi g
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

tef p=
	0.25
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

tef c=
	0.075
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

tef f=
	0.025
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

mt=
	( degc p + depc p ) * dp +
	depc f * df +
	depc c * dc
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

activ time=
	IF THEN ELSE( read from data = 1, activ time data , activ time param )
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

activ time data
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

activ time param=
	0
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

acteff=
	1 + ateff * at
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

acteng bw=
	acteng bw b * ( 1 - 0.652218 * activ time )
	~	kcal/(g*Day)
	~		|

acteng bw at=
	acteng bw * acteff
	~	kcal/(g*Day)
	~		|

at= INTEG (
	atf,
		0)
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

pae=
	acteng bw at * bw
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

tc=
	0.8
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

nacteng bw=
	acteng bw / acteng bw b
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

atf=
	( tc * ndmei - at ) / del at
	~	1/Day
	~		|

acteng bw b=
	0.0256755
	~	kcal/(g*Day)
	~		|

ateff=
	0.52
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

ndmei=
	( mei - mei b ) / mei b
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

del at=
	7
	~	Day
	~		|

lean=
	bm b + ecw + cell mass
	~	g
	~		|

mbc=
	rmr lean * ( cell mass - massb ) + rmr b b * massb + rmr f b * f
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

cell mass=
	ics + c + p + icw
	~	g
	~		|

rmr lean b=
	0.0239374
	~	kcal/(g*Day)
	~		|

rmreff=
	1 + ( 1 - ateff ) * at
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

rmr f b=
	0.0045
	~	kcal/(g*Day)
	~		|

rmr b b=
	0.24
	~	kcal/g/Day
	~		|

rmr lean=
	rmr lean b * rmreff
	~	kcal/g/Day
	~		|

bw=
	f + lean
	~	g
	~		|

massb=
	1400
	~	g
	~		|

depc f=
	0.176744
	~	kcal/g
	~		|

degc p=
	0.172727
	~	kcal/g
	~		|

depc p=
	0.863636
	~	kcal/g
	~		|

depc c=
	0.211111
	~	kcal/g
	~		|

eff obes df=
	(f / f b)^(2/3)
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

k lip=
	LN( ( lipol max - lipol min ) /
	( 1 - lipol min )
	)
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

df mol b=
	0.16
	~	mol/Day
	~		|

ndf=
	eff ci df * eff obes df
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

lipol min=
	0.9
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

lipol max=
	3.1
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

nc=
	c / c b
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

ndc=
	dc / dc b
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

dc=
	dc b * c / c b
	~	g/Day
	~		|

dp=
	dp b * p / p b
	~	g/Day
	~		|

dc b=
	180
	~	g/Day
	~		|

ndp=
	dp / dp b
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

massaa=
	110
	~	g/mol
	~		|

dp b=
	dp mol b * massaa
	~	g/Day
	~		|

dp mol b=
	2.73
	~	mol/Day
	~		|

tee=
	pae + rmr + tef
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

ecw=
	ecw b
	~	g
	~		|

hp=
	2
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

hc=
	2.7
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

ics=
	3967.28
	~	g
	~		|

icw=
	hc * c + hp * p + ciw
	~	g
	~		|

ciw=
	 fiew * ecw b - ( hc * c init + hp * p init)
	~	g
	~		|

fi g=
	fi k / cal f
	~	g/Day
	~		|

ci g  = 
	ci k / cal c
	~	g/Day
	~		|

pi g  = 
	pi k / cal p
	~	g/Day
	~		|

bw b=
	70000
	~	g
	~		|

bm b=
	0.04 * bw b
	~	g
	~		|

ci b=
	ci 0
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

ecw b=
	fw * fetw * bw b
	~	g
	~		|

f b=
	bw b - lean b
	~	g
	~		|

fi b=
	fi 0
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

c b=
	400
	~	g
	~		|

lean b=
	bm b + ecw b + cell mass b
	~	g
	~		|

mei b=
	ci b + fi b +pi b
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

p b=
	cell mass b - icw b - ics - c b
	~	g
	~		|

pi b=
	pi 0
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

molar caloric dens glycerol=
	cal c * mass of glycerol
	~	kcal/mol
	~		|

cal c=
	4.18
	~	kcal/g
	~		|

cal f=
	9.44
	~	kcal/g
	~		|

cal p=
	4.7
	~	kcal/g
	~		|

ci k=
	IF THEN ELSE( read from data = 1,Carbohydrate Intake Data , ci input )
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

Carbohydrate Intake Data
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

ci input=
	1500
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

Protein Intake Data
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

pi input=
	500
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

fi k=
	IF THEN ELSE( read from data = 1, Fat Intake Data , fi input )
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

Fat Intake Data
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

fi input=
	1000
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

protein fraction of cell mass=
	0.2
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

molar caloric dens tg=
	cal f * mass tg
	~	kcal/mol
	~		|

mass tg=
	860
	~	g/mol
	~		|

mass ffa=
	( cal f * mass tg - cal c * mass of glycerol ) / ( 3 * cal f)
	~	g/mol
	~		|

mei=
	ci k + fi k + pi k
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

read from data=
	0
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

mass of glycerol=
	92
	~	g/mol
	~		|

pi k=
	IF THEN ELSE( read from data = 1, Protein Intake Data , pi input )
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

fc=
	carb term / z
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

ff=
	fat term / z
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

fp=
	prot term / z
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

TIME STEP  = 1

c init=
	400
	~	
	~		|

p init=
	8757
	~	
	~		|

f init=
	5075
	~	
	~		|

kf=
	( fi 0 + dnl b - gngf b ) / see b
	~	
	~		|

kp=
	( pi 0 - gngp b ) / see b
	~	
	~		|

gngf b=
	gngf end b + gngf ex b
	~	
	~		|

fetw=
	3/8
	~	
	~		|

cell mass b=
	1/fwcm * icw b
	~	
	~		|

fiew=
	(1-fetw)/fetw
	~	
	~		|

gngf ex b=
	exog glycerol per kcal fat intake * fi 0 * cal c
	~	
	~		|

see b=
	tee b - gngp b - gngf b
	~	
	~		|

pi 0=
	500
	~	
	~		|

eff c dnl b=
	1 / ( k dnl ^ hill dnl + 1 )
	~	
	~		|

fwcm=
	7/10
	~	
	~		|

ci 0=
	1500
	~	
	~		|

tee b=
	mei b
	~	
	~		|

fw=
	7/10
	~	
	~		|

dnl b=
	ci 0 * eff c dnl b
	~	
	~		|

z check 0=
	1+wpi+wci+wg+wf
	~	
	~		|

icw b=
	fiew * ecw b
	~	
	~		|

z check 1=
	wf/kf
	~	
	~		|

fi 0=
	1000
	~	
	~		|

kc=
	( ci 0 - dnl b ) / see b
	~	
	~		|

eff fox p= WITH LOOKUP (
	fox p / fox d,
		([(0,0)-(3,1)],(0,0),(0.4,0.4),(0.798165,0.627193),(1.30275,0.824561),(2,0.95),(3,1\
		) ))
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

fox p=
	f / TIME STEP * cal f
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

fox a=
	fox d / cal f * eff fox p
	~	g/Day
	~		|

pox s=
	fp s * gap / cal p
	~	g/Day
	~		|

pox s k=
	pox s * cal p
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

fox s k=
	fox s * cal f
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

ox=
	ox p + ox s
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

cox s=
	fc s * gap / cal c
	~	g/Day
	~		|

cox s k=
	cox s * cal c
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

fox s=
	ff s * gap / cal f
	~	g/Day
	~		|

d ox tee=
	IF THEN ELSE( ox - tee < 0.1, 0, ox - tee )
	~	kcal/Day [0,0.1]
	~		|

ox s=
	cox s k + fox s k + pox s k
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

y=
	prot term + is sufficient carb * carb term + is sufficient fat * fat term
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

fc s=
	is sufficient carb * carb term / y
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

ff s=
	is sufficient fat * fat term / y
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

fp s=
	prot term / y
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

is sufficient fat=
	IF THEN ELSE( gap f < 0.1 , 1 , 0 )
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

is sufficient carb=
	IF THEN ELSE( gap c < 0.1 , 1, 0 )
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

cox a=
	cox d / cal c * eff suff c
	~	g/Day
	~		|

cox d=
	fc * see + gngf + gngp
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

suff c=
	c * cal c / cox d
	~	Day
	~		|

eff suff c= WITH LOOKUP (
	suff c,
		([(0,0)-(1,1),(0,0),(0.1,0.6),(0.2,0.85),(0.3,0.95),(0.4,1),(1,1)],(0,0),(0.1,0.6),\
		(0.2,0.85),(0.3,0.95),(0.4,1),(1,1) ))
	~	Dmnl
	~	\!suff c
	|

gap=
	gap c + gap f
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

f= INTEG (
	+fi g-fox a+dnl i-gngf o-fox s,
		f init)
	~	g
	~		|

c= INTEG (
	ci g+gngf i+gngp i-cox a-dnl o-cox s,
		c init)
	~	g
	~		|

gap c=
	cox d - cox a * cal c
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

gap f=
	fox d - fox a * cal f
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

cox k=
	cox a * cal c
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

p= INTEG (
	pi g-gngp o-pox a-pox s,
		p init)
	~	g
	~		|

fox k=
	fox a * cal f
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

pox k=
	pox a * cal p
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

ox p=
	cox k + fox k + pox k
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

ec=
	-268
	~	kcal/Day
	~	double counted baseline metabolic activity
	|

rmr=
	mbc + mt + mc + ec
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

z=
	carb term + fat term +prot term
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

wf=
	(1 + wpi) * kf / kp
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

fat term=
	MAX( 0 , wf * ndf)
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

wg=
	kc / kp * ( 1 + wpi )- wci
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

eff dg cox=
	wg * ndc
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

eff act pox=
	sa * EXP( - LN(sa) * nacteng bw )
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

spi=
	15.0253
	~	Dmnl
	~	Makalede bu degiken 7.
	|

sa=
	4
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

eff pi pox=
	wpi * ( 1 + spi * ndpi )
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

eff ci cox=
	wci * ( 1 + sci * ndci )
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

wpi=
	0.1
	~	Dmnl
	~	relative rate of exogenous to endogenous protein in balanced state (from \
		model)
	|

prot term=
	( ndp + MAX( 0, eff pi pox )  ) * eff act pox
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

sci=
	0.761188
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

wci=
	3.31414
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

carb term=
	eff dg cox + MAX( 0 , eff ci cox * ( c / (0.1 + c) )  )
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

dnleff=
	0.8
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

gngeff=
	0.8
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

mc=
	( 1 - dnleff ) * dnl + ( 1- gngeff ) * ( gngf + gngp )
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

see=
	tee - gngp - gngf
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

dnl=
	ci g * eff c dnl * cal c
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

dnl o=
	min( dnl / cal c , c / TIME STEP )
	~	g/Day
	~		|

pox d=
	fp * see
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

gngf=
	gngf end + gngf ex
	~	
	~		|

fox d=
	ff * see
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

gngf i=
	gngf / cal c
	~	g/Day
	~		|

gngf o=
	min( gngf / cal f , f / TIME STEP )
	~	g/Day
	~		|

gngp o=
	MAX( 0 , gngp / cal p)
	~	g/Day
	~		|

dnl i=
	dnl / cal f
	~	g/Day
	~		|

gngp=
	MAX( 0 , gngp b * ( np - eff ci gngp + eff pi gngp ) )
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

eff ci gngp=
	0.506 * ndci
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

gngp i=
	gngp / cal c
	~	g/Day
	~		|

pox a=
	pox d / cal p
	~	g/Day
	~		|

gngf end b=
	df mol b * mass of glycerol * cal c
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

gngf end=
	gngf end b * ndf
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

gngf ex=
	exog glycerol per kcal fat intake * fi k * cal c
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

exog glycerol per kcal fat intake=
	mass of glycerol / ( cal f * mass tg )
	~	g/kcal
	~		|

hill dnl=
	4
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

k dnl=
	2
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

eff c dnl=
	nc ^ hill dnl / 
	( k dnl ^ hill dnl + nc ^ hill dnl )
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

dci=
	ci k - ci b
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

ndci=
	dci / ci b
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

ndpi=
	dpi / pi b
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

np=
	p / p b
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

dpi=
	pi k - pi b
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

eff pi gngp=
	0.306 * ndpi
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

gngp b=
	100
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

eff ci df=
	1 + ( ( lipol max - lipol min )  * EXP( -k lip * ci g * cal c / ci b )
	+ lipol min - 1 )
	/ MAX( 1 , eff obes df )
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

df=
	df mol b * ndf * mass tg
	~	g/Day
	~		|

tef=
	tef c * cal c * ci g + tef f * fi k + tef p * cal p * pi g
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

tef p=
	0.25
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

tef c=
	0.075
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

tef f=
	0.025
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

mt=
	( degc p + depc p ) * dp +
	depc f * df +
	depc c * dc
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

activ time=
	IF THEN ELSE( read from data = 1, activ time data , activ time param )
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

activ time data
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

activ time param=
	0
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

acteff=
	1 + ateff * at
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

acteng bw=
	acteng bw b * ( 1 - 0.652218 * activ time )
	~	kcal/(g*Day)
	~		|

acteng bw at=
	acteng bw * acteff
	~	kcal/(g*Day)
	~		|

at= INTEG (
	atf,
		0)
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

pae=
	acteng bw at * bw
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

tc=
	0.8
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

nacteng bw=
	acteng bw / acteng bw b
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

atf=
	( tc * ndmei - at ) / del at
	~	1/Day
	~		|

acteng bw b=
	0.0256755
	~	kcal/(g*Day)
	~		|

ateff=
	0.52
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

ndmei=
	( mei - mei b ) / mei b
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

del at=
	7
	~	Day
	~		|

lean=
	bm b + ecw + cell mass
	~	g
	~		|

mbc=
	rmr lean * ( cell mass - massb ) + rmr b b * massb + rmr f b * f
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

cell mass=
	ics + c + p + icw
	~	g
	~		|

rmr lean b=
	0.0239374
	~	kcal/(g*Day)
	~		|

rmreff=
	1 + ( 1 - ateff ) * at
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

rmr f b=
	0.0045
	~	kcal/(g*Day)
	~		|

rmr b b=
	0.24
	~	kcal/g/Day
	~		|

rmr lean=
	rmr lean b * rmreff
	~	kcal/g/Day
	~		|

bw=
	f + lean
	~	g
	~		|

massb=
	1400
	~	g
	~		|

depc f=
	0.176744
	~	kcal/g
	~		|

degc p=
	0.172727
	~	kcal/g
	~		|

depc p=
	0.863636
	~	kcal/g
	~		|

depc c=
	0.211111
	~	kcal/g
	~		|

eff obes df=
	(f / f b)^(2/3)
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

k lip=
	LN( ( lipol max - lipol min ) /
	( 1 - lipol min )
	)
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

df mol b=
	0.16
	~	mol/Day
	~		|

ndf=
	eff ci df * eff obes df
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

lipol min=
	0.9
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

lipol max=
	3.1
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

nc=
	c / c b
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

ndc=
	dc / dc b
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

dc=
	dc b * c / c b
	~	g/Day
	~		|

dp=
	dp b * p / p b
	~	g/Day
	~		|

dc b=
	180
	~	g/Day
	~		|

ndp=
	dp / dp b
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

massaa=
	110
	~	g/mol
	~		|

dp b=
	dp mol b * massaa
	~	g/Day
	~		|

dp mol b=
	2.73
	~	mol/Day
	~		|

tee=
	pae + rmr + tef
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

ecw=
	ecw b
	~	g
	~		|

hp=
	2
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

hc=
	2.7
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

ics=
	3967.28
	~	g
	~		|

icw=
	hc * c + hp * p + ciw
	~	g
	~		|

ciw=
	 fiew * ecw b - ( hc * c init + hp * p init)
	~	g
	~		|

fi g=
	fi k / cal f
	~	g/Day
	~		|

ci g  = 
	ci k / cal c
	~	g/Day
	~		|

pi g  = 
	pi k / cal p
	~	g/Day
	~		|

bw b=
	70000
	~	g
	~		|

bm b=
	0.04 * bw b
	~	g
	~		|

ci b=
	ci 0
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

ecw b=
	fw * fetw * bw b
	~	g
	~		|

f b=
	bw b - lean b
	~	g
	~		|

fi b=
	fi 0
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

c b=
	400
	~	g
	~		|

lean b=
	bm b + ecw b + cell mass b
	~	g
	~		|

mei b=
	ci b + fi b +pi b
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

p b=
	cell mass b - icw b - ics - c b
	~	g
	~		|

pi b=
	pi 0
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

molar caloric dens glycerol=
	cal c * mass of glycerol
	~	kcal/mol
	~		|

cal c=
	4.18
	~	kcal/g
	~		|

cal f=
	9.44
	~	kcal/g
	~		|

cal p=
	4.7
	~	kcal/g
	~		|

ci k=
	IF THEN ELSE( read from data = 1,Carbohydrate Intake Data , ci input )
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

Carbohydrate Intake Data
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

ci input=
	1500
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

Protein Intake Data
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

pi input=
	500
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

fi k=
	IF THEN ELSE( read from data = 1, Fat Intake Data , fi input )
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

Fat Intake Data
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

fi input=
	1000
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

protein fraction of cell mass=
	0.2
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

molar caloric dens tg=
	cal f * mass tg
	~	kcal/mol
	~		|

mass tg=
	860
	~	g/mol
	~		|

mass ffa=
	( cal f * mass tg - cal c * mass of glycerol ) / ( 3 * cal f)
	~	g/mol
	~		|

mei=
	ci k + fi k + pi k
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

read from data=
	0
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

mass of glycerol=
	92
	~	g/mol
	~		|

pi k=
	IF THEN ELSE( read from data = 1, Protein Intake Data , pi input )
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

fc=
	carb term / z
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

ff=
	fat term / z
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

fp=
	prot term / z
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

c init=
	400
	~	
	~		|

p init=
	8757
	~	
	~		|

f init=
	5075
	~	
	~		|

kf=
	( fi 0 + dnl b - gngf b ) / see b
	~	
	~		|

kp=
	( pi 0 - gngp b ) / see b
	~	
	~		|

gngf b=
	gngf end b + gngf ex b
	~	
	~		|

fetw=
	3/8
	~	
	~		|

cell mass b=
	1/fwcm * icw b
	~	
	~		|

fiew=
	(1-fetw)/fetw
	~	
	~		|

gngf ex b=
	exog glycerol per kcal fat intake * fi 0 * cal c
	~	
	~		|

see b=
	tee b - gngp b - gngf b
	~	
	~		|

pi 0=
	500
	~	
	~		|

eff c dnl b=
	1 / ( k dnl ^ hill dnl + 1 )
	~	
	~		|

fwcm=
	7/10
	~	
	~		|

ci 0=
	1500
	~	
	~		|

tee b=
	mei b
	~	
	~		|

fw=
	7/10
	~	
	~		|

dnl b=
	ci 0 * eff c dnl b
	~	
	~		|

z check 0=
	1+wpi+wci+wg+wf
	~	
	~		|

icw b=
	fiew * ecw b
	~	
	~		|

z check 1=
	wf/kf
	~	
	~		|

fi 0=
	1000
	~	
	~		|

kc=
	( ci 0 - dnl b ) / see b
	~	
	~		|

eff fox p= WITH LOOKUP (
	fox p / fox d,
		([(0,0)-(3,1)],(0,0),(0.4,0.4),(0.798165,0.627193),(1.30275,0.824561),(2,0.95),(3,1\
		) ))
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

fox p=
	f / TIME STEP * cal f
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

fox a=
	fox d / cal f * eff fox p
	~	g/Day
	~		|

pox s=
	fp s * gap / cal p
	~	g/Day
	~		|

pox s k=
	pox s * cal p
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

fox s k=
	fox s * cal f
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

ox=
	ox p + ox s
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

cox s=
	fc s * gap / cal c
	~	g/Day
	~		|

cox s k=
	cox s * cal c
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

fox s=
	ff s * gap / cal f
	~	g/Day
	~		|

d ox tee=
	IF THEN ELSE( ox - tee < 0.1, 0, ox - tee )
	~	kcal/Day [0,0.1]
	~		|

ox s=
	cox s k + fox s k + pox s k
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

y=
	prot term + is sufficient carb * carb term + is sufficient fat * fat term
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

fc s=
	is sufficient carb * carb term / y
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

ff s=
	is sufficient fat * fat term / y
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

fp s=
	prot term / y
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

is sufficient fat=
	IF THEN ELSE( gap f < 0.1 , 1 , 0 )
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

is sufficient carb=
	IF THEN ELSE( gap c < 0.1 , 1, 0 )
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

cox a=
	cox d / cal c * eff suff c
	~	g/Day
	~		|

cox d=
	fc * see + gngf + gngp
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

suff c=
	c * cal c / cox d
	~	Day
	~		|

eff suff c= WITH LOOKUP (
	suff c,
		([(0,0)-(1,1),(0,0),(0.1,0.6),(0.2,0.85),(0.3,0.95),(0.4,1),(1,1)],(0,0),(0.1,0.6),\
		(0.2,0.85),(0.3,0.95),(0.4,1),(1,1) ))
	~	Dmnl
	~	\!suff c
	|

gap=
	gap c + gap f
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

f= INTEG (
	+fi g-fox a+dnl i-gngf o-fox s,
		f init)
	~	g
	~		|

c= INTEG (
	ci g+gngf i+gngp i-cox a-dnl o-cox s,
		c init)
	~	g
	~		|

gap c=
	cox d - cox a * cal c
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

gap f=
	fox d - fox a * cal f
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

cox k=
	cox a * cal c
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

p= INTEG (
	pi g-gngp o-pox a-pox s,
		p init)
	~	g
	~		|

fox k=
	fox a * cal f
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

pox k=
	pox a * cal p
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

ox p=
	cox k + fox k + pox k
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

ec=
	-268
	~	kcal/Day
	~	double counted baseline metabolic activity
	|

rmr=
	mbc + mt + mc + ec
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

z=
	carb term + fat term +prot term
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

wf=
	(1 + wpi) * kf / kp
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

fat term=
	MAX( 0 , wf * ndf)
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

wg=
	kc / kp * ( 1 + wpi )- wci
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

eff dg cox=
	wg * ndc
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

eff act pox=
	sa * EXP( - LN(sa) * nacteng bw )
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

spi=
	15.0253
	~	Dmnl
	~	Makalede bu degiken 7.
	|

sa=
	4
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

eff pi pox=
	wpi * ( 1 + spi * ndpi )
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

eff ci cox=
	wci * ( 1 + sci * ndci )
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

wpi=
	0.1
	~	Dmnl
	~	relative rate of exogenous to endogenous protein in balanced state (from \
		model)
	|

prot term=
	( ndp + MAX( 0, eff pi pox )  ) * eff act pox
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

sci=
	0.761188
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

wci=
	3.31414
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

carb term=
	eff dg cox + MAX( 0 , eff ci cox * ( c / (0.1 + c) )  )
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

dnleff=
	0.8
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

gngeff=
	0.8
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

mc=
	( 1 - dnleff ) * dnl + ( 1- gngeff ) * ( gngf + gngp )
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

see=
	tee - gngp - gngf
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

dnl=
	ci g * eff c dnl * cal c
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

dnl o=
	min( dnl / cal c , c / TIME STEP )
	~	g/Day
	~		|

pox d=
	fp * see
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

gngf=
	gngf end + gngf ex
	~	
	~		|

fox d=
	ff * see
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

gngf i=
	gngf / cal c
	~	g/Day
	~		|

gngf o=
	min( gngf / cal f , f / TIME STEP )
	~	g/Day
	~		|

gngp o=
	MAX( 0 , gngp / cal p)
	~	g/Day
	~		|

dnl i=
	dnl / cal f
	~	g/Day
	~		|

gngp=
	MAX( 0 , gngp b * ( np - eff ci gngp + eff pi gngp ) )
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

eff ci gngp=
	0.506 * ndci
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

gngp i=
	gngp / cal c
	~	g/Day
	~		|

pox a=
	pox d / cal p
	~	g/Day
	~		|

gngf end b=
	df mol b * mass of glycerol * cal c
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

gngf end=
	gngf end b * ndf
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

gngf ex=
	exog glycerol per kcal fat intake * fi k * cal c
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

exog glycerol per kcal fat intake=
	mass of glycerol / ( cal f * mass tg )
	~	g/kcal
	~		|

hill dnl=
	4
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

k dnl=
	2
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

eff c dnl=
	nc ^ hill dnl / 
	( k dnl ^ hill dnl + nc ^ hill dnl )
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

dci=
	ci k - ci b
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

ndci=
	dci / ci b
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

ndpi=
	dpi / pi b
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

np=
	p / p b
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

dpi=
	pi k - pi b
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

eff pi gngp=
	0.306 * ndpi
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

gngp b=
	100
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

eff ci df=
	1 + ( ( lipol max - lipol min )  * EXP( -k lip * ci g * cal c / ci b )
	+ lipol min - 1 )
	/ MAX( 1 , eff obes df )
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

df=
	df mol b * ndf * mass tg
	~	g/Day
	~		|

tef=
	tef c * cal c * ci g + tef f * fi k + tef p * cal p * pi g
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

tef p=
	0.25
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

tef c=
	0.075
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

tef f=
	0.025
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

mt=
	( degc p + depc p ) * dp +
	depc f * df +
	depc c * dc
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

activ time=
	IF THEN ELSE( read from data = 1, activ time data , activ time param )
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

activ time data
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

activ time param=
	0
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

acteff=
	1 + ateff * at
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

acteng bw=
	acteng bw b * ( 1 - 0.652218 * activ time )
	~	kcal/(g*Day)
	~		|

acteng bw at=
	acteng bw * acteff
	~	kcal/(g*Day)
	~		|

at= INTEG (
	atf,
		0)
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

pae=
	acteng bw at * bw
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

tc=
	0.8
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

nacteng bw=
	acteng bw / acteng bw b
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

atf=
	( tc * ndmei - at ) / del at
	~	1/Day
	~		|

acteng bw b=
	0.0256755
	~	kcal/(g*Day)
	~		|

ateff=
	0.52
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

ndmei=
	( mei - mei b ) / mei b
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

del at=
	7
	~	Day
	~		|

lean=
	bm b + ecw + cell mass
	~	g
	~		|

mbc=
	rmr lean * ( cell mass - massb ) + rmr b b * massb + rmr f b * f
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

cell mass=
	ics + c + p + icw
	~	g
	~		|

rmr lean b=
	0.0239374
	~	kcal/(g*Day)
	~		|

rmreff=
	1 + ( 1 - ateff ) * at
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

rmr f b=
	0.0045
	~	kcal/(g*Day)
	~		|

rmr b b=
	0.24
	~	kcal/g/Day
	~		|

rmr lean=
	rmr lean b * rmreff
	~	kcal/g/Day
	~		|

bw=
	f + lean
	~	g
	~		|

massb=
	1400
	~	g
	~		|

depc f=
	0.176744
	~	kcal/g
	~		|

degc p=
	0.172727
	~	kcal/g
	~		|

depc p=
	0.863636
	~	kcal/g
	~		|

depc c=
	0.211111
	~	kcal/g
	~		|

eff obes df=
	(f / f b)^(2/3)
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

k lip=
	LN( ( lipol max - lipol min ) /
	( 1 - lipol min )
	)
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

df mol b=
	0.16
	~	mol/Day
	~		|

ndf=
	eff ci df * eff obes df
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

lipol min=
	0.9
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

lipol max=
	3.1
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

nc=
	c / c b
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

ndc=
	dc / dc b
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

dc=
	dc b * c / c b
	~	g/Day
	~		|

dp=
	dp b * p / p b
	~	g/Day
	~		|

dc b=
	180
	~	g/Day
	~		|

ndp=
	dp / dp b
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

massaa=
	110
	~	g/mol
	~		|

dp b=
	dp mol b * massaa
	~	g/Day
	~		|

dp mol b=
	2.73
	~	mol/Day
	~		|

tee=
	pae + rmr + tef
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

ecw=
	ecw b
	~	g
	~		|

hp=
	2
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

hc=
	2.7
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

ics=
	3967.28
	~	g
	~		|

icw=
	hc * c + hp * p + ciw
	~	g
	~		|

ciw=
	 fiew * ecw b - ( hc * c init + hp * p init)
	~	g
	~		|

fi g=
	fi k / cal f
	~	g/Day
	~		|

ci g  = 
	ci k / cal c
	~	g/Day
	~		|

pi g  = 
	pi k / cal p
	~	g/Day
	~		|

bw b=
	70000
	~	g
	~		|

bm b=
	0.04 * bw b
	~	g
	~		|

ci b=
	ci 0
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

ecw b=
	fw * fetw * bw b
	~	g
	~		|

f b=
	bw b - lean b
	~	g
	~		|

fi b=
	fi 0
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

c b=
	400
	~	g
	~		|

lean b=
	bm b + ecw b + cell mass b
	~	g
	~		|

mei b=
	ci b + fi b +pi b
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

p b=
	cell mass b - icw b - ics - c b
	~	g
	~		|

pi b=
	pi 0
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

molar caloric dens glycerol=
	cal c * mass of glycerol
	~	kcal/mol
	~		|

cal c=
	4.18
	~	kcal/g
	~		|

cal f=
	9.44
	~	kcal/g
	~		|

cal p=
	4.7
	~	kcal/g
	~		|

ci k=
	IF THEN ELSE( read from data = 1,Carbohydrate Intake Data , ci input )
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

Carbohydrate Intake Data
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

ci input=
	1500
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

Protein Intake Data
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

pi input=
	500
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

fi k=
	IF THEN ELSE( read from data = 1, Fat Intake Data , fi input )
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

Fat Intake Data
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

fi input=
	1000
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

protein fraction of cell mass=
	0.2
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

molar caloric dens tg=
	cal f * mass tg
	~	kcal/mol
	~		|

mass tg=
	860
	~	g/mol
	~		|

mass ffa=
	( cal f * mass tg - cal c * mass of glycerol ) / ( 3 * cal f)
	~	g/mol
	~		|

mei=
	ci k + fi k + pi k
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

read from data=
	0
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

mass of glycerol=
	92
	~	g/mol
	~		|

pi k=
	IF THEN ELSE( read from data = 1, Protein Intake Data , pi input )
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

fc=
	carb term / z
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

ff=
	fat term / z
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

fp=
	prot term / z
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

c init=
	400
	~	
	~		|

p init=
	8757
	~	
	~		|

f init=
	5075
	~	
	~		|

kf=
	( fi 0 + dnl b - gngf b ) / see b
	~	
	~		|

kp=
	( pi 0 - gngp b ) / see b
	~	
	~		|

gngf b=
	gngf end b + gngf ex b
	~	
	~		|

fetw=
	3/8
	~	
	~		|

cell mass b=
	1/fwcm * icw b
	~	
	~		|

fiew=
	(1-fetw)/fetw
	~	
	~		|

gngf ex b=
	exog glycerol per kcal fat intake * fi 0 * cal c
	~	
	~		|

see b=
	tee b - gngp b - gngf b
	~	
	~		|

pi 0=
	500
	~	
	~		|

eff c dnl b=
	1 / ( k dnl ^ hill dnl + 1 )
	~	
	~		|

fwcm=
	7/10
	~	
	~		|

ci 0=
	1500
	~	
	~		|

tee b=
	mei b
	~	
	~		|

fw=
	7/10
	~	
	~		|

dnl b=
	ci 0 * eff c dnl b
	~	
	~		|

z check 0=
	1+wpi+wci+wg+wf
	~	
	~		|

icw b=
	fiew * ecw b
	~	
	~		|

z check 1=
	wf/kf
	~	
	~		|

fi 0=
	1000
	~	
	~		|

kc=
	( ci 0 - dnl b ) / see b
	~	
	~		|

eff fox p= WITH LOOKUP (
	fox p / fox d,
		([(0,0)-(3,1)],(0,0),(0.4,0.4),(0.798165,0.627193),(1.30275,0.824561),(2,0.95),(3,1\
		) ))
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

fox p=
	f / TIME STEP * cal f
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

fox a=
	fox d / cal f * eff fox p
	~	g/Day
	~		|

pox s=
	fp s * gap / cal p
	~	g/Day
	~		|

pox s k=
	pox s * cal p
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

fox s k=
	fox s * cal f
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

ox=
	ox p + ox s
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

cox s=
	fc s * gap / cal c
	~	g/Day
	~		|

cox s k=
	cox s * cal c
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

fox s=
	ff s * gap / cal f
	~	g/Day
	~		|

d ox tee=
	IF THEN ELSE( ox - tee < 0.1, 0, ox - tee )
	~	kcal/Day [0,0.1]
	~		|

ox s=
	cox s k + fox s k + pox s k
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

y=
	prot term + is sufficient carb * carb term + is sufficient fat * fat term
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

fc s=
	is sufficient carb * carb term / y
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

ff s=
	is sufficient fat * fat term / y
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

fp s=
	prot term / y
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

is sufficient fat=
	IF THEN ELSE( gap f < 0.1 , 1 , 0 )
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

is sufficient carb=
	IF THEN ELSE( gap c < 0.1 , 1, 0 )
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

cox a=
	cox d / cal c * eff suff c
	~	g/Day
	~		|

cox d=
	fc * see + gngf + gngp
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

suff c=
	c * cal c / cox d
	~	Day
	~		|

eff suff c= WITH LOOKUP (
	suff c,
		([(0,0)-(1,1),(0,0),(0.1,0.6),(0.2,0.85),(0.3,0.95),(0.4,1),(1,1)],(0,0),(0.1,0.6),\
		(0.2,0.85),(0.3,0.95),(0.4,1),(1,1) ))
	~	Dmnl
	~	\!suff c
	|

gap=
	gap c + gap f
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

f= INTEG (
	+fi g-fox a+dnl i-gngf o-fox s,
		f init)
	~	g
	~		|

c= INTEG (
	ci g+gngf i+gngp i-cox a-dnl o-cox s,
		c init)
	~	g
	~		|

gap c=
	cox d - cox a * cal c
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

gap f=
	fox d - fox a * cal f
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

cox k=
	cox a * cal c
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

p= INTEG (
	pi g-gngp o-pox a-pox s,
		p init)
	~	g
	~		|

fox k=
	fox a * cal f
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

pox k=
	pox a * cal p
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

ox p=
	cox k + fox k + pox k
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

ec=
	-268
	~	kcal/Day
	~	double counted baseline metabolic activity
	|

rmr=
	mbc + mt + mc + ec
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

z=
	carb term + fat term +prot term
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

wf=
	(1 + wpi) * kf / kp
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

fat term=
	MAX( 0 , wf * ndf)
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

wg=
	kc / kp * ( 1 + wpi )- wci
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

eff dg cox=
	wg * ndc
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

eff act pox=
	sa * EXP( - LN(sa) * nacteng bw )
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

spi=
	15.0253
	~	Dmnl
	~	Makalede bu degiken 7.
	|

sa=
	4
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

eff pi pox=
	wpi * ( 1 + spi * ndpi )
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

eff ci cox=
	wci * ( 1 + sci * ndci )
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

wpi=
	0.1
	~	Dmnl
	~	relative rate of exogenous to endogenous protein in balanced state (from \
		model)
	|

prot term=
	( ndp + MAX( 0, eff pi pox )  ) * eff act pox
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

sci=
	0.761188
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

wci=
	3.31414
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

carb term=
	eff dg cox + MAX( 0 , eff ci cox * ( c / (0.1 + c) )  )
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

dnleff=
	0.8
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

gngeff=
	0.8
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

mc=
	( 1 - dnleff ) * dnl + ( 1- gngeff ) * ( gngf + gngp )
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

see=
	tee - gngp - gngf
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

dnl=
	ci g * eff c dnl * cal c
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

dnl o=
	min( dnl / cal c , c / TIME STEP )
	~	g/Day
	~		|

pox d=
	fp * see
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

gngf=
	gngf end + gngf ex
	~	
	~		|

fox d=
	ff * see
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

gngf i=
	gngf / cal c
	~	g/Day
	~		|

gngf o=
	min( gngf / cal f , f / TIME STEP )
	~	g/Day
	~		|

gngp o=
	MAX( 0 , gngp / cal p)
	~	g/Day
	~		|

dnl i=
	dnl / cal f
	~	g/Day
	~		|

gngp=
	MAX( 0 , gngp b * ( np - eff ci gngp + eff pi gngp ) )
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

eff ci gngp=
	0.506 * ndci
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

gngp i=
	gngp / cal c
	~	g/Day
	~		|

pox a=
	pox d / cal p
	~	g/Day
	~		|

gngf end b=
	df mol b * mass of glycerol * cal c
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

gngf end=
	gngf end b * ndf
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

gngf ex=
	exog glycerol per kcal fat intake * fi k * cal c
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

exog glycerol per kcal fat intake=
	mass of glycerol / ( cal f * mass tg )
	~	g/kcal
	~		|

hill dnl=
	4
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

k dnl=
	2
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

eff c dnl=
	nc ^ hill dnl / 
	( k dnl ^ hill dnl + nc ^ hill dnl )
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

dci=
	ci k - ci b
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

ndci=
	dci / ci b
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

ndpi=
	dpi / pi b
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

np=
	p / p b
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

dpi=
	pi k - pi b
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

eff pi gngp=
	0.306 * ndpi
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

gngp b=
	100
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

eff ci df=
	1 + ( ( lipol max - lipol min )  * EXP( -k lip * ci g * cal c / ci b )
	+ lipol min - 1 )
	/ MAX( 1 , eff obes df )
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

df=
	df mol b * ndf * mass tg
	~	g/Day
	~		|

tef=
	tef c * cal c * ci g + tef f * fi k + tef p * cal p * pi g
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

tef p=
	0.25
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

tef c=
	0.075
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

tef f=
	0.025
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

mt=
	( degc p + depc p ) * dp +
	depc f * df +
	depc c * dc
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

activ time=
	IF THEN ELSE( read from data = 1, activ time data , activ time param )
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

activ time data
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

activ time param=
	0
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

acteff=
	1 + ateff * at
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

acteng bw=
	acteng bw b * ( 1 - 0.652218 * activ time )
	~	kcal/(g*Day)
	~		|

acteng bw at=
	acteng bw * acteff
	~	kcal/(g*Day)
	~		|

at= INTEG (
	atf,
		0)
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

pae=
	acteng bw at * bw
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

tc=
	0.8
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

nacteng bw=
	acteng bw / acteng bw b
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

atf=
	( tc * ndmei - at ) / del at
	~	1/Day
	~		|

acteng bw b=
	0.0256755
	~	kcal/(g*Day)
	~		|

ateff=
	0.52
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

ndmei=
	( mei - mei b ) / mei b
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

del at=
	7
	~	Day
	~		|

lean=
	bm b + ecw + cell mass
	~	g
	~		|

mbc=
	rmr lean * ( cell mass - massb ) + rmr b b * massb + rmr f b * f
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

cell mass=
	ics + c + p + icw
	~	g
	~		|

rmr lean b=
	0.0239374
	~	kcal/(g*Day)
	~		|

rmreff=
	1 + ( 1 - ateff ) * at
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

rmr f b=
	0.0045
	~	kcal/(g*Day)
	~		|

rmr b b=
	0.24
	~	kcal/g/Day
	~		|

rmr lean=
	rmr lean b * rmreff
	~	kcal/g/Day
	~		|

bw=
	f + lean
	~	g
	~		|

massb=
	1400
	~	g
	~		|

depc f=
	0.176744
	~	kcal/g
	~		|

degc p=
	0.172727
	~	kcal/g
	~		|

depc p=
	0.863636
	~	kcal/g
	~		|

depc c=
	0.211111
	~	kcal/g
	~		|

eff obes df=
	(f / f b)^(2/3)
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

k lip=
	LN( ( lipol max - lipol min ) /
	( 1 - lipol min )
	)
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

df mol b=
	0.16
	~	mol/Day
	~		|

ndf=
	eff ci df * eff obes df
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

lipol min=
	0.9
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

lipol max=
	3.1
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

	c / c b
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

ndc=
	dc / dc b
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

dc=
	dc b * c / c b
	~	g/Day
	~		|

dp=
	dp b * p / p b
	~	g/Day
	~		|

dc b=
	180
	~	g/Day
	~		|

	dp / dp b
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

	110
	~	g/mol
	~		|

	~	g/Day
	~		|

	2.73
	~	mol/Day
	~		|

	pae + rmr + tef
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

ecw=

	~	g
	~		|

	2
	~	Dmnl
	~		|

	2.7
	~	Dmnl

	3967.28
	~	g
	~		|

	~	g
	~		|

	~	g
	~		|

	fi k / cal f
	~	g/Day
	~		|

	ci k / cal c
	~	g/Day
	~		|

	~	g/Day
	~		|

bw b=
	70000
	~	g
	~		|

	~	g
	~		|

	ci 0
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

	~	g

	~	g

	~	g

	pi 0
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

	~	kcal/mol

	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

Fat Intake Data
	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

fi input=

	~	kcal/Day
	~		|

protein fraction of cell mass=
	0.2
	~	Dmnl

read from data=

	~	kcal/Day
